STAT table

STAT table

Info

Khand Light Regular (Khand-Light.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Info

Khand Regular (Khand-Regular.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Khand Light Regular (Khand-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Khand' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Khand Light'.

Pass

MS NID 6

Khand Medium Regular (Khand-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Khand' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Khand Medium'.

Mac NID 6

NID 6 is 'Khand-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Khand SemiBold Regular (Khand-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Khand' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Khand SemiBold'.

Pass
